Conference of the Parties
Twenty-second session
Marrakech, 7–18 November 2016


           List of participants

           Part one

           Parties
           Afghanistan – Maldives

                   The attached list of participants attending the twenty-second session of the
           Conference of the Parties, the twelfth session of the Conference of the Parties serving as the
           meeting of the Parties to the Kyoto Protocol and the first session of the Conference of the
           Parties serving as the meeting of the Parties to the Paris Agreement, as well as the forty-
           fifth sessions of the subsidiary bodies, has been prepared on the basis of information
           received by the secretariat as at Wednesday, 16 November 2016.
